<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прогулять.html>прогуля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proguljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***прогуливаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прогуливаться.html>прогу́ливаться</a> (8452)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прогуливать.html>прогу́ливать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">progúlivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прогуливаться.html>прогу́ливаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">progúlivatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прогуляться.html>прогуля́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take a walk/stroll, to promenade
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пойти́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прогуливаться.html>прогу́ливаться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pojtí <b>progúlivatʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">go for a walk/stroll</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to stroll, to saunter, to ramble</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прогуливать.html>прогу́ливать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">progúlivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прогулка.html>прогу́лка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">progúlka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гулять.html>гуля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">guljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прогулять.html>прогуля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proguljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прогуляться.html>прогуля́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proguljátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прогуливаться.html>прогу́ливаться</a></b>)

<li>to stroll, to saunter, to ramble</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продать.html>прода́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продавать.html>продава́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodavátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продаваться.html>продава́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodavátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продаться.html>прода́ться</a></b>)
</p>

<li>to sell oneself, to betray</li>

***продавить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продавить.html>продави́ть</a> (19123)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">davítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продавить.html>продави́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodavítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прода́вливать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crush/break through, to squeeze/press through</li>
<li><i>(seat, sofa etc)</i> to cause to sink [sag down]
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:диван.html>дива́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:продавленный.html>прода́влен</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">diván prodávlen</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the sofa sags down</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press <i>(for)</i>, to ram, to win, to bring off, to put across, to push <i>(through)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:правительство.html>прави́тельство</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:продавить.html>продави́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поправка.html>попра́вки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закон.html>зако́ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:парламент.html>парла́мент</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pravítelʹstvo <b>prodavílo</b> poprávki k zakónu čerez parláment</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the cabinet rammed/railroaded/pushed the amendments to the law through parliament</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давить.html>дави́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">davítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раздавить.html>раздави́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razdavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задавить.html>задави́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zadavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***продажа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продажа.html>прода́жа</a> (2668)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:продажа.html>прода́жа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodaža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prodaďa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продажа.html>прода́жа</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodáža</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продажа.html>прода́жи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продажа.html>прода́жи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продажа.html>прода́ж</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sale, selling (exchange of goods or services for currency or credit)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:продажа.html>прода́жу</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>prodážu</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">for sale</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продажность.html>прода́жность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodážnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продажность.html>прода́жности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продажность.html>прода́жности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продажность.html>прода́жностей</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продажа.html>прода́жа</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodáža</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продажный.html>прода́жный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodážnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)прода́жнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)прода́жней</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прода́жнейший</b>)

***продать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продать.html>прода́ть</a> (1676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дать.html>дать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">datʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li>to sell</li>
<li>to sell out, to betray</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продаться.html>прода́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prodátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продаваться.html>продава́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prodavátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продвигавший.html>продвигавший</a> (25737)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвигавший.html>продвига́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodvigávšij</span>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвигать.html>продвига́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodvigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle_2">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвигавший.html>продви́гавший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodvígavšij</span>)

***продвигать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продвигать.html>продви́гать</a> (25737)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">продви́г-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodvíg-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвигать.html>продвига́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodvigátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвинуть.html>продви́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move <i>or</i> to push ahead (on, forward, further)</li>
<li>to promote, to advance, to further <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to encourage growth</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двигать.html>дви́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvígatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвигать.html>продви́гать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodvígatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двигать.html>дви́гать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spend some time moving (something)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вчера.html>вчера́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>весь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:продвигать.html>продви́гали</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мебель.html>ме́бель</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Včerá my vesʹ denʹ <b>prodvígali</b> mébelʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Yesterday we <b>spent</b> the whole day <b>moving</b> furniture.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***продвигаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продвигаться.html>продвига́ться</a> (7336)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвигать.html>продвига́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodvigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвигаться.html>продвига́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodvigátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвинуться.html>продви́нуться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to advance, to move/push forward/on/further, to gain/make ground, to make headway
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>боя́ми</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:продвигаться.html>продвига́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вперед.html>вперёд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s bojámi <b>prodvigátʹsja</b> vperjód</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fight one's way forward</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:продвигаться.html>продвига́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скачка.html>скачка́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prodvigátʹsja</b> skačkámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to progress in fits and starts</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to advance, to make progress/headway</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвигать.html>продвига́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodvigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продвинуть.html>продви́нуть</a> (18869)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:двинуть.html>дви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвинуть.html>продви́нуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodvínutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвигать.html>продвига́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to move <i>or</i> to push ahead (on, forward, further)</li>
<li>to promote, to advance, to further <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to encourage growth</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<li>поспособствовать <a href = vnd.unilang:распространение.html>распростране́нию</a> какой-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:продукция.html>проду́кции</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:услуга.html>услу́ги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рынок.html>ры́нке</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сбыт.html>сбыта</a> <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>

</ol>

***продвинуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:продвинуться.html>продви́нуться</a> (11396)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвинуть.html>продви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвинуться.html>продви́нуться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prodvínutʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвигаться.html>продвига́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to advance, to move/push forward/on/further, to gain/make ground, to make headway
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бой.html>боя́ми</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:продвинуться.html>продви́нуться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вперед.html>вперёд</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s bojámi <b>prodvínutʹsja</b> vperjód</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fight one's way forward</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:продвинуться.html>продви́нуться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скачка.html>скачка́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prodvínutʹsja</b> skačkámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to progress in fits and starts</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to advance, to make progress/headway</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:продвинуть.html>продви́нуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prodvínutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
